<DESCRIPTION>NEWSLETTER DATED JULY 23, 2015

<HTML>
<HEAD>
     <TITLE></TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0; text-align: right; margin-bottom: 0; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; background-color: white"><B>Exhibit
99.1</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; background-color: white"><B><I>&nbsp;</I></B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; background-color: white"><B><I>A
Letter from the CEO</I></B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; background-color: white"><B><I>July
2015</I></B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; background-color: white"><B>Dear
Shareholder and/or Supporter,</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; background-color: white">Zion
Oil and Gas, Inc. (&ldquo;Zion&rdquo; or &ldquo;Company&rdquo; NASDAQ: ZN), is a publicly traded oil and gas exploration company
dedicated to finding oil and gas onshore Israel. I believe that by faith (Heb. 11:1) and diligent professional work we are in
the best position ever to see exploration success.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">We
have been following news items that negatively affect our economy such as Greece&rsquo;s financial default and the Iranian nuclear
deal. Further downward pressure on the price of oil is also negatively affecting oil and gas exploration efforts but we&rsquo;d
like to focus more on <B>Zion&rsquo;s positive potential</B> as we continue to work toward drilling our next exploratory well
late this year or early in 2016.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; background-color: white">We
held our Annual Shareholder and Board of Directors Meeting in Dallas on </FONT><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">June
10-11, 2015<FONT STYLE="background-color: white">. Several key corporate issues were decided, including </FONT>stockholder approval
to increase the number of shares of common stock that the Company is authorized to issue from 100 million to 200 million shares.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">Following
our annual shareholder meeting, the Board of Directors named Mr. Glen Perry as our new President and Chief Operating Officer and
me as Zion&rsquo;s new CEO. Mr. John Brown, the Company&rsquo;s founder, will continue to serve as Executive Chairman of our Board
of Directors. He will also continue to provide our Biblical vision, advise me in my new role as CEO, and be involved in key company
initiatives such as developing the Good News from Zion project.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

Zion Oil &amp; Gas Board of Directors</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; background-color: white">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; background-color: white">I
wholeheartedly welcome the new challenges and responsibilities as Zion&rsquo;s CEO and seek your continued prayer and support
for God&rsquo;s guidance and wisdom to help us achieve exploration success. As a result of ongoing evaluation of previous and
newly acquired geological and geophysical data, our exploration focus is now wholly concentrated on our <B>99,000 acre onshore
Megiddo-Jezreel License</B>.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; background-color: white"><B>MEGIDDO
- JEZREEL LICENSE</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; background-color: white">Our
Megiddo-Jezreel License area appears to possess the key geologic ingredients of an active petroleum system with significant onshore
exploration potential. </FONT><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">This license gives Zion the <B>exclusive
right to explore</B> in a large area of approximately 99,000 acres. <FONT STYLE="background-color: white">We have now met yet
another critical milestone by delivering to the Energy Ministry our 100<SUP>+</SUP> page </FONT><B>Megiddo-Jezreel #1 Well Drilling
Prospect Report</B> in compliance with the terms of our license.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; background-color: white">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="color: #222222; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; background-color: white">We
have selected the precise drill pad location from which to drill our next well(s). Multiple wells could be drilled from this pad
site as several subsurface geologic targets can be reached using directional well trajectories. Zion is well into the process
of </FONT><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">gaining official approval of our <FONT STYLE="background-color: white">comprehensive
Environmental Impact Assessment (EIA) study documents. </FONT>Study topics included: ecology, geology, hydrology (water), archaeology,
acoustics, air quality, hazardous materials, pollution, land reclamation, drilling methods, risk mitigation, etc.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

are a few key 2015 milestones:</FONT></P>
